 isliye duniyabar main vibhinn bhugolic sthitiyon main kaisar ke swaroop or failaav main bhinnata najar aati he

 uski vajah se hi ye yah bhranti failati he ki cancer laailaaj he

 use badalane ke liye drudh rajnatik or prashasnic sankalp kii jarurat he
 Going through the ups and downs of life and during different circumstances in the last nearly 35 years, whenever people came to know about my profession, first of all, some common questions have been flying in the air, like - what is cancer? Is it contagious? It is necessary to state here that cancer is not an infectious disease, and eating, sleeping or drinking with a cancer patient does not spread this disease
 kai log ise khandaani beemaari maanate hai
 But there are some cancer diseases that can be seen in various members due to family history, eating habits or other reasons
 inamen colon cancer he jo khan-paan kii aadaton se hota he
 Breast cancer can occur due to genetic reasons in mother and daughter
 sirf 5 fisadi cancer janetic hote hai
 Cancer is an uncontrolled, irregular and abnormal growth of cells that can begin from any part of the body, tissue or organ, perhaps for some known or or hitherto unknown reason
 yah shuruaati kaaran khatm ho jane ke baad bhi jari rah sakati he, jisaki pravriti aas-paas ke saamaanya utakon main ghuspaith karne or raktavahikaaon main ghus jane kii he, jisase yah rog fefdon, liver, dimag or haddiyon jaise kuch angon yaa puure sharir ke hisson main fail jaataa he

 agar ilaaj na ho to aakhirkaar rogi kii maut ho jaati he
